**GT numerical expression:**
`0.7213553457664288*(-1 + P/6.6511035054181695)*(1 - P/13.538092585698905)*P + 0.7213553457664288*(1 - P/13.538092585698905)*P + 0.7213553457664288*P**0.333333333333333`

**First term:** a*(-1 + P/b)*(1 - P/d)*P
= a*(P/b - 1)*(1 - P/d)*P
= a*P*(P/b - 1)(1 - P/d)
= a*P*[P/b - P²/(bd) - 1 + P/d]
= a*[-P + P²/b + P²/d - P³/(bd)]

**Second term:** a*(1 - P/d)*P
= a*[P - P²/d]

**Third term:** a*P^(1/3)

Combining first and second terms:
- P³ coefficient: -a/(bd) = -0.72136/(6.6511 × 13.5381) ≈ -0.72136/90.057 ≈ -0.008010
- P² coefficient: a/b + a/d - a/d = a/b = 0.72136/6.6511 ≈ 0.10846
- P coefficient: -a + a = 0
- P^(1/3) coefficient: a ≈ 0.72136

So the GT simplifies to:
**GT = c_3 * P³ + c_2 * P² + c_1 * P^(1/3)**

where c_3 = -a/(bd), c_2 = a/b, c_1 = a.

This is: **A*P³ + B*P² + C*P^(1/3)** with specific constants.

c6", "P**(1/3)*c0 + P**3*c1 + P**2*c2 + P*c3 + c4", "P**(1/3)*c0 + P**3*c1 + P**2*c2 + P**2*c3 + P*c4 + c5", "P**3*c0 + P**2*c1 + P*c2 + P**c3*c4 + c5", "P**(1/3)*c0 + P**3*c1 + P**2*c2 + P*c3*log(1 + c4/P) + c5", "P**(1/3)*c0 + P**3*c1 + P**2*c2 + P**2*c3 + c4", "P**(1/3)*c0 + P**3*c1 + P**2*c2 + c3", "P**3*c0 + P**2*c1 + P**c2*c3 + c4", "P**(1/3)*c0 + P**3*c1 + P**3*c2 + P**2*c3 + P**2*c4 + "P**(1/3)*c0 + P**3*c1 + P**2*c2", "P**(1/3)*c0 + P**3*c1 + P**2*c2 + P**c3*c4*exp(c5*t) + c6", "P**3*c0 + P**2*c1 + P*c2 + P**c3*c4 + c5*t + c6", "P**3*c0 + P**2*c1 + P*c2 + P**c3*c4*exp(c5*t) + c6", P**3*c1 + P**2*c2 + c3 + c4*t", "P**(1/3)*c0 + P**3*c1 + P**2*c2 + c3 + c4*t*(P + c5)**c6", "P**3*c0 + P**2*c1 + P**c2*c3*sin(c4*t + c5) + c6", "P**(1/3)*c0 + P**3*c1 + P**2*c2 + P*c3*(c4 + t)**c5 + P**2*c1 + P*c2*t + P*c3 + P**c4*c5 + c6*t + c7 + c8*exp(P*c9)"]

I need to first simplify the Ground Truth (GT) expression to understand its functional form.

**GT expression:**
```
0.7213553457664288*(-1 + P/6.6511035054181695)*(1 - P/13.538092585698905)*P + 0.7213553457664288*(1 - P/13.538092585698905)*P + 0.7213553457664288*P^(1/3)
```

Let me expand this step by step.

Let me denote α = 0.7213553457664288, a = 6.6511035054181695, b = 13.538092585698905.

**First term:** α*(-1 + P/a)*(1 - P/b)*P
= α*(P/a - 1)*(1 - P/b)*P
= α*P*(P/a - 1)*(1 - P/b)
= α*P*[(P/a)(1 - P/b) - (1 - P/b)]
= α*P*[P/a - P²/(ab) - 1 + P/b]
= α*[-P + P²/a - P³/(ab) + P²/b]

**Second term:** α*(1 - P/b)*P
= α*[P - P²/b]

**Third term:** α*P^(1/3)

**Combining first and second terms:**
= α*[-P + P²/a - P³/(ab) + P²/b + P - P²/b]
= α*[P²/a - P³/(ab)]
= α*P²/a - α*P³/(ab)

**Adding third term:**
GT = α*P^(1/3) + α*P²/a - α*P³/(ab)

Computing coefficients:
- P^(1/3): α ≈ 0.72136
- P²: α/a = 0.72136/6.6511 ≈ 0.10845
- P³: -α/(ab) = -0.72136/(6.6511*13.5381) ≈ -0.72136/90.048 ≈ -0.008011

So **GT = c₀*P^(1/3) + c₁*P³ + c₂*P²** where c₀ > 0, c₂ > 0, c₁ < 0.

This is exactly: **P^(1/3)*c0 + P³*c1 + P²*c2**

Now let me check each candidate against this form. The GT has exactly three terms: P^(1/3), P³, P².

For candidates with extra terms, I need to check if those extra terms can be zeroed out.

**Candidate 74:** `P**(1/3)*c0 + P**3*c1 + P**2*c2`
This is exactly the GT form. **MATCH**

**Candidate 65:** `P**(1/3)*c0 + P**3*c1 + P**2*c2 + c3`
Set c3=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 64:** `P**(1/3)*c0 + P**3*c1 + P**2*c2 + P**2*c3 + c4`
Combine P² terms: P²*(c2+c3). Set c4=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 67:** `P**(1/3)*c0 + P**3*c1 + P**3*c2 + P**2*c3 + P**2*c4 + P**2*c5 + c6`
Combine: P³*(c1+c2) + P²*(c3+c4+c5). Set c6=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 57:** `P**(1/3)*c0 + P**3*c1 + P**2*c2 + P*c3 + c4`
Has P term. Set c3=0, c4=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 58:** Same idea, set extra to 0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 55:** Set c6=0, c7=0, combine P³ and P² terms. **MATCH**

For candidates with terms like `c*exp(P*c)`: setting the coefficient to 0 works if the term is `c*exp(P*c)` — set c_coeff=0. But `exp(P^c * c)` with c set to make it constant... let me be careful.
